 Katra is the Bais Camp of Mata Vaishno Devi, 50 km away from Jammu
 vaishno devi mandir jane vaale shraddhalu yaheen se hokar guzarate hai
 There are several ways to cover the 13-kilometer route from Katra to Mata's temple
 aap chahen to paidal ja sakate hai
 The second way is that you can reach for darshan of the mother by sitting on a horse or a tattoo

 The reason for the murder is not yet clear
 police ne aaropee ko hiraasat main le liya he
 The incident is in the Maruti Kunj area of cyber city
 jahaan beeti der raat ajay naamak ek shaks ne apni 27 varshiya patni sandhya kii cabel vir se galaa ghontkarnirmam hatyakar di
 The evening of the deceased was 7 months pregnant
 soochna milane par police maukey par pahunchi or panchnaame kii karrwai ke baad shav ko postmortem ke liye bhej diya

 ab police usase katl kii vajah ke silsile main poochtacha kar rahi he

 aaropee ajay maaruti kunj main hi bijli maikenic kaa kaam karata he
 Initial investigations revealed that there was often a fight between the two
 baharhaal police abhi maamle kii tafteesh main juty he

 In fact, after the Reserve Bank of India (RBI) order, the country's largest bank, the State Bank of India has removed the charges on NEFT and RTGS from 1 July
 RBI dwaara digital lenden ko badhaava dene ke uddeshy se len-dein par lagane vaale shulkon ko khatm kiya ja rahaa he
 In this series, the bank has now decided to withdraw the fee from August 1 on making transactions with IMPS (tatkal Payment Service)
 gauratlab he ki badi raashi ke lenden ke liye RTGS or do lakh rupee tak ke lenden ke liye NEFT pranali kaa upyog kiya jaataa he
 The bank says that users transferring funds via YONO, internet banking and mobile banking will no longer be charged any IMPS
 SBI graahakon ke liye ek tarah se yah badi raahat he
 Now no fee will be charged on IMPS transactions as well
 yono (you only nid van) bank kii digital or lifestil manchon ko ek saath laane vaali ap kaa naam he
 Its registered customers number around 10 million
 esbiai ke 6 karod internet baking graahak hai, jabaki 1
 41 crore people use mobile banking
 bank ke digital plateform yono ko 1 karod graahak istemaal karte hai
 What happens IMPS is an instant interbank electronic fund transfer service of the Intermediate Payment Service (IMPS), which is done through other channels such as mobile phones and atms, Internet banking

 ab jammu main bhi asaram ke khilaaf jaanch shuru hogi

 adaalat ne police ko nae sire se jaanch kaa nirdesh diya he

 asaram ke hi kareebi rahe bholanandar naam ke ek shaks ne daawa kiya tha ki teenon bacchon kii rahasyamayi haalat main maut ke baad shavon ko ashram ke parisar main hi dafna diya gaya tha
 Following this revelation, an NGO had requested the court to investigate the matter
 bholanand ne yah daawa kiya tha ki unhone asaram ke jammu sthit ashram main kareeb saat saal kaam kiya tha
 During this time, three children died under mysterious circumstances in the ashram of Jammu, after which those three children were buried in the ashram premises itself
 itnaa hi nahin bholanand ne yah bhi daawa kiya tha ki agar use police kii suraksha main jammu ke ashram le jaaya gaya to wo us jagah kii bhi pahchaan bhi kar legaa jahaan in bacchon ko dafnaaya gaya tha
